 Ballot papers, not electronic voting machines (evms), will be used in presidential elections because this is an election in which every elector has to register his first and second priority
 raashtrapati chunaav main upyog kiye jane vaale mataptr main koi chunaav chihn nahin hota
 There are only two columns, the first column contains the names of the candidates and the second column is empty, in which the elector has to write his preferences
 duusare chunaavon main matadaata apni pasand ke ummidavaar ke liye keval ek vot daalata he magar raashtrapati chunaav main nirvaachak ko apni praathamikta bataane ke liye ummidavaaron ke naam ke aage 1 yaa 2 likhnaa hota he
 In the presidential election, a four-day gap has to be kept between the voting and the declaration of the result
 isliye ki matpetiyon ko vibhinn rajyon se dilli laayaa jaataa he
 Members of the Legislative Assembly vote in the states
 gyaat ho ki raashtrapati chunaav guuruuvaar ko hoga or matganana ravivaar ko hogi
 Members of Parliament can either vote in Delhi or in the Legislative Assembly of the state from which they are elected
 iske liye lekin unhen purvanumati leni padati he
 In the first round of counting, only the first priority votes are counted
 jo ummidavaar 50 fisadi se adhik mat hasil kar letaa he, use vijayi ghoshit kiya jaataa he
 If the first round counting does not make it clear who the winner is, then the second round votes are counted in the second round and the winner is declared by combining the votes of both rounds
 tippaniyan They have the right to vote in the presidential elections who are elected members of Lok Sabha, Rajya Sabha or State Legislative Assembly
 manonith sadasyon ko raashtrapati chunane kaa haq nahin hota
 The total number of those electing the president is 4,896, including 776 mps and 4,120 mlas
 in sabhi ke mat 10,97,000 maton ke baraabar hai
 The ballot used in the presidential election has no election mark
 keval do kollam hote hai, pehle kollam main ummidavaaron ke naam hote hai or doosraa kollam khaali rahata he, jisamen nirvaachak ko apni praathamiktaayen likhni hoti he
 In the second election, the voter casts only one vote for the candidate of their choice, but in the presidential election, the elector has to write 1 or 2 in front of the candidate's name to indicate their preference
 raashtrapati chunaav main matdaan or parinaam kii ghoshnaa ke bich chaar din kaa faasla rakhana padataa he
 Because ballots are brought to Delhi from various states
 rajyon main vidhansabha ke sadsy matdaan karte hai
 It is to be known that the presidential election will be held on Thursday and the counting of votes will take place on Sunday
 sansad sadsy yaa to dilli main matdaan kar sakate hai yaa us rajya kii vidhansabha main, jahaan se ve nirvaachit hue hai
 For this, they have to take prior permission
 pehle daur kii matganana main keval pehali praathamikta vaale maton kii ginati hoti he
 The candidate who gets more than 50 percent of the vote is declared victorious
 pehle daur kii matganana se yadi spasht nahin ho paata ki vijeta koun he, tab duusare daur main duusari praathamikta vaale maton kii ginati hoti he or donon daur ke maton ko jodakar vijeta kii ghoshnaa kii jaati he
 The comments raashtrapati chunaav main matdaan karne kaa adhikaar unhen praapt he jo loksabhaa, rajyasabha yaa rajya vidhansabha ke nirvaachit sadsy hai
 The nominated members are not entitled to elect the President

 1
 Vinegar is a wonderful cheese, black and red colored tiles become dirtier than other tiles
